              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-CZ34x9ws9MY/VZ9tz74g_UI/AAAAAAAAX_4/TW2H2QPpPk8/s1600/IMG_2501.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-CZ34x9ws9MY/VZ9tz74g_UI/AAAAAAAAX_4/TW2H2QPpPk8/s640/IMG_2501.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 As my pile grew
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I stacked them into this
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 vintage Pyrex bowl:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-5WF7411AYJg/VZ9t3818m6I/AAAAAAAAYAA/GK3dQQOLkHA/s1600/Image%2B4.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-5WF7411AYJg/VZ9t3818m6I/AAAAAAAAYAA/GK3dQQOLkHA/s640/Image%2B4.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 They eventually turned into
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 the
                </span>
               </b>
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 borders and alternate
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 blocks for this quilt...
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yXe5DVh3seU/VZ9t-ai5zYI/AAAAAAAAYAI/nWAPASYcwuk/s1600/Image%2B8.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-yXe5DVh3seU/VZ9t-ai5zYI/AAAAAAAAYAI/nWAPASYcwuk/s640/Image%2B8.jpg" width="426"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: x-large;">
                 Scrappy Haystack Sampler
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 on page 132 of my book.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-aRfC8MhV3-A/VZ9z1dbYK3I/AAAAAAAAYBA/6Bn0O1c8Fd4/s1600/IMG_2167.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-aRfC8MhV3-A/VZ9z1dbYK3I/AAAAAAAAYBA/6Bn0O1c8Fd4/s640/IMG_2167.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 It's a nice queen size
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 and I love how it looks on my bed:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Q1OmLQ4S1do/VZ9uLnoataI/AAAAAAAAYAY/KKHFNTn00SI/s1600/Image%2B43.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Q1OmLQ4S1do/VZ9uLnoataI/AAAAAAAAYAY/KKHFNTn00SI/s640/Image%2B43.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I used several
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 12" farm girl blocks to alternate
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 between the haystack blocks...
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Ycgsd3qMVjw/VZ9uPNfp5WI/AAAAAAAAYAg/W52FXj1jnDw/s1600/Image%2B45.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Ycgsd3qMVjw/VZ9uPNfp5WI/AAAAAAAAYAg/W52FXj1jnDw/s640/Image%2B45.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 If you are making my
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Scrappy Haystack Sampler too
                </span>
               </b>
               <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                <b>
                 
                </b>
               </span>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 here are just a few to choose from:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mxQKlaK--o8/VZ9uTXkDfmI/AAAAAAAAYAo/5AYZltbyXGw/s1600/IMG_6450.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mxQKlaK--o8/VZ9uTXkDfmI/AAAAAAAAYAo/5AYZltbyXGw/s640/IMG_6450.JPG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 There are 45 farm girl
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 blocks total in my book:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: x-large;">

                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LVK9p5PwS0w/VZ9uY0RZH-I/AAAAAAAAYAw/NOE2EQ3WxRQ/s640/Image%2B70.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

         <div class="date-outer">
          <h2 class="date-header">
           <span>
            Friday, July 3, 2015
           </span>
          </h2>
          <div class="date-posts">
           <div class="post-outer">
            <div class="post hentry uncustomized-post-template">
             <a name="7575429504743876608">
             </a>
             <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
              <a href="http://beeinmybonnetco.blogspot.com/2015/07/farm-girl-friday-week-ten.html">
               Farm Girl Friday - Week Ten! ...
              </a>
             </h3>
             <div class="post-header-line-1">
             </div>
             <div class="post-body entry-content">
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-e5wjR4BCvD0/VZYr_jKZhbI/AAAAAAAAX8E/oYwlpN0bsDc/s1600/Image%2B5.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="426" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-e5wjR4BCvD0/VZYr_jKZhbI/AAAAAAAAX8E/oYwlpN0bsDc/s640/Image%2B5.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Good morning!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 It's time for another episode of
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Farm Girl Fridays!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Today we are talking about my
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: x-large;">
                 Gingham Block
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 This was one of the
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 very first blocks to design
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 for the book
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 gingham is classic farm girl style
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 and you all know how much I love my gingham:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Someday I'll be making a big quilt
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 just from my gingham blocks
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 but for right now
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I'm happy with my gingham runner!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">

              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-1C-4vLZcHbM/VZYs0m9dXpI/AAAAAAAAX8Y/G7DUytOSTYU/s1600/IMG_2293.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-1C-4vLZcHbM/VZYs0m9dXpI/AAAAAAAAX8Y/G7DUytOSTYU/s640/IMG_2293.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I love how it looks on my table.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I made the centerpieces by painting
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 4 large tomato sauce cans and
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 then wrapping them in burlap and lace.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I put a vintage milk bottle in each can
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 and put daisies in each one.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 A simple farm girl style project!
                </span>

               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Instructions for my Gingham block
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 are on page 36 of my book

              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: x-large;">
                 Farm Girl Vintage
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 If you want to join our sew along
                </span>

               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 to grab a copy and get started!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <b>
               <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                <br/>
               </span>
              </b>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-n2Qam80UwtM/VZYq6SrLw7I/AAAAAAAAX7M/2vrRntBguNE/s1600/Image%2B10.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-n2Qam80UwtM/VZYq6SrLw7I/AAAAAAAAX7M/2vrRntBguNE/s640/Image%2B10.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I decided to make a cute little project
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 starting with the 12" Gingham block:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 A tip about choosing fabric for this block
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 is that you need to make sure that
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 there is plenty of contrast between
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 the two colors
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 otherwise you will lose the gingham look:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <b>
               <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                <br/>
               </span>
              </b>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NPsl2KvN2xk/VZYq9Uvrh4I/AAAAAAAAX7U/MbLv3M-WOiQ/s1600/Image%2B11.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">

                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                </span>

                 I started out by cutting
                </span>
               </b>

                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Or insert the pillow form and
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 have a super cute pillow!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <b>
               <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                <br/>
               </span>
              </b>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YYEmr9njT-A/VZYrMjyePpI/AAAAAAAAX78/F-RGFbNF36g/s1600/Image%2B8.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YYEmr9njT-A/VZYrMjyePpI/AAAAAAAAX78/F-RGFbNF36g/s640/Image%2B8.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Every farm girl kitchen
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 should have a gingham pillow:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Ozgr6sy2NA8/VZaMDNHZuqI/AAAAAAAAX8o/uKyjRWKRIjs/s1600/Image%2B5.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="636" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Ozgr6sy2NA8/VZaMDNHZuqI/AAAAAAAAX8o/uKyjRWKRIjs/s640/Image%2B5.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Next farm girl block
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 for this week is on page 35 and is my
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: x-large;">
                 Furrows Block
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Another classic and super simple one.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I chose to make scrappy flying geese
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 and name the block Furrows
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 to represent the look of a pasture after
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 it's just been plowed and ready for planting!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-n96w7Ozap5g/VZaMGZhCd8I/AAAAAAAAX8w/4oYGJszO_NY/s1600/Image%2B15.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-n96w7Ozap5g/VZaMGZhCd8I/AAAAAAAAX8w/4oYGJszO_NY/s640/Image%2B15.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Last night I decided to whip up a few 12" Furrows blocks.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I grabbed my 3 1/2" scrappy stash basket
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 and quickly cut some geese:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DV_rLKFr6jI/VZaMI3WFqZI/AAAAAAAAX84/DGs21rWYeDc/s1600/Image%2B16.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DV_rLKFr6jI/VZaMI3WFqZI/AAAAAAAAX84/DGs21rWYeDc/s640/Image%2B16.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Chain pieced them...
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uyxOLG_6D7E/VZaML6S-SVI/AAAAAAAAX9A/C5aF0yGHWYM/s1600/Image%2B17.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uyxOLG_6D7E/VZaML6S-SVI/AAAAAAAAX9A/C5aF0yGHWYM/s640/Image%2B17.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 And soon they were ready to be sewn into
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: x-large;">
                 Furrows
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace;">
                 (background is Swiss Dots by Riley Blake in Navy)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-SBLt-4mMoAE/VZaMOpyN9lI/AAAAAAAAX9I/CKT0gXlTJtw/s1600/Image%2B18.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-SBLt-4mMoAE/VZaMOpyN9lI/AAAAAAAAX9I/CKT0gXlTJtw/s640/Image%2B18.jpg" width="638"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I made 9 blocks and laid them out on the floor
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 for placement auditions.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Each block represents a plowed pasture.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I turned each block a different direction and
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 now I have 9 scrappy happy acres
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 plowed and ready for planting!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I could easily add more blocks to this quilt
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 but I just may stop here because a
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 36" square quilt would be a super cute table topper!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-s2Dht_Zze3E/VZaMa3b4P4I/AAAAAAAAX9Q/hzBsQV_YWs8/s1600/IMG_5409.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="626" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-s2Dht_Zze3E/VZaMa3b4P4I/AAAAAAAAX9Q/hzBsQV_YWs8/s640/IMG_5409.PNG" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Thanks for joining me for week ten
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 of my Farm Girl Fridays Sew Along...
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HWEloY6cA2w/VZaMe74JCpI/AAAAAAAAX9Y/JHfFA_5K_dM/s1600/Image%2B1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="102" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HWEloY6cA2w/VZaMe74JCpI/AAAAAAAAX9Y/JHfFA_5K_dM/s640/Image%2B1.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: x-large;">
                 <a href="http://fatquartershop.blogspot.com/p/farm-girl-vintage-sew-along.html">
                  CLICK HERE
                 </a>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 to see the schedule and to
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 visit this weeks guest bloggers!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Now go put on some
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 gingham and plow your fields!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">

          <h2 class="date-header">
           <span>
            Friday, June 26, 2015
           </span>
          </h2>
          <div class="date-posts">
           <div class="post-outer">
            <div class="post hentry uncustomized-post-template">
             <a name="974921191959127192">
             </a>
             <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
              <a href="http://beeinmybonnetco.blogspot.com/2015/06/farm-girl-friday-week-nine.html">
               Farm Girl Friday - Week Nine!
              </a>
             </h3>
             <div class="post-header-line-1">
             </div>
             <div class="post-body entry-content">
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-0yZ5N0XO3Hs/VYq677v3vvI/AAAAAAAAX4M/PQiR6V6lQMw/s1600/Image%2B3.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="632" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-0yZ5N0XO3Hs/VYq677v3vvI/AAAAAAAAX4M/PQiR6V6lQMw/s640/Image%2B3.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Good morning cute people!
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Welcome to week nine of
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Farm Girl Fridays:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">

              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I made a big stack of 12" blocks
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 because I am making a few pear projects:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-uxRw6atGHQc/VYq7wjJSA-I/AAAAAAAAX5s/x6VT6cpVvr0/s1600/Image%2B1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-uxRw6atGHQc/VYq7wjJSA-I/AAAAAAAAX5s/x6VT6cpVvr0/s640/Image%2B1.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I made 16 total because I need 12 to make the
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 County Fair Quilt Setting on page 112...
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-2U3kjiYGTGk/VYq7zXJ5YPI/AAAAAAAAX50/cJEbSXkunuw/s1600/Image%2B3.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-2U3kjiYGTGk/VYq7zXJ5YPI/AAAAAAAAX50/cJEbSXkunuw/s640/Image%2B3.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 And I'm using the remaining 4 to make
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 a pillow for the bench in my kitchen:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Hx_yeHJwYNU/VYq717UgDXI/AAAAAAAAX58/O4gnbFYAgM4/s1600/Image%2B2.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Hx_yeHJwYNU/VYq717UgDXI/AAAAAAAAX58/O4gnbFYAgM4/s640/Image%2B2.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I haven't decided how I'm setting the
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 blocks for the pillow yet
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 but I'm sure that when I finish it
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I will be posting lots of pics on my
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: x-large;">
                 <a href="https://instagram.com/beelori1/">
                  Instagram!
                 </a>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZXhQmdPH59k/VYq75xz-03I/AAAAAAAAX6E/yBYwjXnNnQk/s1600/Image.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="294" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZXhQmdPH59k/VYq75xz-03I/AAAAAAAAX6E/yBYwjXnNnQk/s640/Image.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>
                </b>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Thank you so much for
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 joining me for this weeks episode:)
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 I am once again away at one of my
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 Farm Girl Vintage Workshop/Retreats
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 but I prepared my post early
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 just for you today.
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <b>
                <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
               </b>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tAKRqISpkT4/VYrHnVderEI/AAAAAAAAX6o/ajTnD8n56Po/s1600/Image%2B1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <b>
                 <span style="font-family: Courier New, Courier, monospace; font-size: large;">
                  <img border="0" height="102" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tAKRqISpkT4/VYrHnVderEI/AAAAAAAAX6o/ajTnD8n56Po/s640/Image%2B1.jpg" width="640"/>
                 </span>

              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

               </b>

        <h2 class="title">
         Grab a button...
        </h2>

       <div class="widget Profile" id="Profile2">
        <h2>
         About the Queen Bee...
        </h2>
        <div class="widget-content">
         <a href="https://plus.google.com/118439591010544568646">
          <img alt="My Photo" class="profile-img" height="80" src="//lh5.googleusercontent.com/-E_HyMStc58k/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAATCM/ZFsr_iBLj9s/s80-c/photo.jpg" width="80"/>
         </a>
         <dl class="profile-datablock">
          <dt class="profile-data">
           <a class="profile-name-link g-profile" href="https://plus.google.com/118439591010544568646" rel="author" style="background-image: url(//www.google.com/images/icons/ui/gprofile_button-16.png);">
            Lori Holt
           </a>
           <br/>
           <div class="g-follow" data-annotation="bubble" data-height="20" data-href="https://plus.google.com/118439591010544568646">
           </div>
          </dt>
          <dd class="profile-textblock">
           You can find me most often in my studio drawing for my next fabric line or creating designs for my pattern company established in 1994 called "Bee in my Bonnet" I'm a small town girl who loves everything vintage.
          </dd>
